     <div class="index-header-content">
      <div class="index-header-content-wrapper">
       <h1>
        Visual &amp; flexible software
        <br/>
        to adopt and scale Agile
       </h1>
       <div class="index-header-tabs">
        <ul class="index-header-tabs-list">
         <li class="current">
          Overview
         </li>
         <li>
          For enterprise
         </li>
         <li>
          For companies
         </li>
         <li>
          For teams
         </li>
        </ul>
        <div class="index-header-tabs-body">
         <p class="index-header-tab-content current">
          Visually manage complex work. Reduce clutter and focus on the things that matter.
  Whether you’re scaling Agile through your entire company or adopting it for the first
  time,
  we’ve got your back. From
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/kanban-for-a-company/">
           Kanban
          </a>
          and
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/scrum-for-a-company/">
           Scrum
          </a>
          to
          <a class="title-link" href="http://safe.targetprocess.com/" target="_blank">
           SAFe
          </a>
          and NEXUS, Targetprocess adapts
  to your
  management approach.
         </p>
         <p class="index-header-tab-content">
          Targetprocess
          <a class="title-link" href="/about/scale-agile-ppm/">
           enables you to scale Agile
          </a>
          across the enterprise using such Agile at scale frameworks as
          <a class="title-link" href="http://safe.targetprocess.com/" target="_blank">
           SAFe
          </a>
          ,
  LeSS, NEXUS, and SoS.
  Connect the dots between execution and strategy by bringing IT work and business goals
  together. Say goodbye to plugins for managing portfolios,
  to intermediary spreadsheets, and to manual synchronization of
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/project-portfolio-management/">
           ALM and PPM
          </a>
          data!
         </p>
         <p class="index-header-tab-content">
          Visibility without clutter. Transparency without overload. Our tool’s visual focus makes
  it easy to plan and execute
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/project-portfolio-management/">
           high level
  strategy
          </a>
          in a
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/developer/">
           team-friendly environment
          </a>
          ,
  without getting bogged down by inflexible processes.
         </p>
         <p class="index-header-tab-content">
          Never lose track of a work item again. See
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/developer/#manage_todo_list_and_track_time">
           all your
  work in one place
          </a>
          and communicate with colleagues without email. Create custom views to show just what is
  relevant for you, and use
          <a class="title-link" href="/solutions/development/#monitor_valuable_metrics">
           graphical and
  custom reports
          </a>
          to help identify trends and forecast performance.
         </p>
        </div>

    <section class="feature-content-section">
     <h2 class="feature-content-main-head">
      Example features
     </h2>
    </section>
    <section class="feature-content-section">
     <article class="content-section">
      <h2>
       Visualization
      </h2>
      <div class="two-sides-content" id="visualization-slider">
       <div class="side">
        <p>
         Targetprocess makes it easy to get a distraction-free overview of your projects, with the
  ability to drill down or scale up for details from any level of the hierarchy.
        </p>
        <div class="features-examples-list">
         <div class="feature-example" data-image="//assets.cdntpondemand.com/content/themes/targetprocess/img/page-features/ex-pic4.png?t=2018728103439" id="timelines-agro">
          <div class="ex-ico">
           <div class="icon">
           </div>
          </div>
          <h4 class="ex-head">
           Timelines
           <span class="ex-count">
            7 examples
           </span>
          </h4>
          <p>
           Plan the future, visualize and track activities, and get a high-level overview of how
  your work progresses over time.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="feature-example" data-image="//assets.cdntpondemand.com/content/themes/targetprocess/img/page-features/ex-pic2.png?t=2018728103439" id="boards-agro">
          <div class="ex-ico">
           <div class="icon">
           </div>
          </div>
          <h4 class="ex-head">
           Boards
           <span class="ex-count">
            10 examples
           </span>
          </h4>
          <p>
           See anything you want as a board. Boards are great for planning and progress
  tracking.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="feature-example" data-image="//assets.cdntpondemand.com/content/themes/targetprocess/img/page-features/ex-pic5.png?t=2018728103439" id="lists-agro">
          <div class="ex-ico">
           <div class="icon">
           </div>
          </div>
          <h4 class="ex-head">
           Lists
           <span class="ex-count">
            6 examples
           </span>
          </h4>
          <p>
           See project hierarchy and manage backlogs with ease. Full customization, inline editing
  and beautiful design.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="side">
        <div class="pic-example" id="features-images-output">
         <img alt="" class="slider-output-image visible" data-src="//assets.cdntpondemand.com/content/themes/targetprocess/img/page-features/ex-pic1.png?t=2018728103439"/>
         <div class="banner">
          <img alt="" src="//assets.cdntpondemand.com/content/themes/targetprocess/img/page-features/banner.svg?t=2018728103439"/>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="plates">
       <div class="plate-line">
        <div class="plate-item">
         <h4 class="plate-head">
          Batch drag and drop
         </h4>
         <div class="plate-ico">
          <div class="el-icon i-16">
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          Select multiple cards and move them into any place you want.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="plate-item">
         <h4 class="plate-head">
          Good Information density
         </h4>
         <div class="plate-ico">
          <div class="el-icon i-0">
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          Filter, zoom, collapse and focus. Boards give you many options for handling large amounts of
  cards seamlessly.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="plate-line">
        <div class="plate-item">
         <h4 class="plate-head">
          Flexibility
         </h4>
         <div class="plate-ico">
          <div class="el-icon i-38">
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          Create various boards. Select card types, horizontal and vertical swimlanes, set default
  sorting, customize card content.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="plate-item">
         <h4 class="plate-head">
          Share boards
         </h4>
         <div class="plate-ico">
          <div class="el-icon i-30">
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          Easily share boards with any person to broadcast information outside.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </article>

    <section class="feature-content-section slider">
     <article class="content-section">
      <div class="head-wrap">
       <h2>
        Custom reports
       </h2>
       <p class="sub-head">
        Build your own dynamic visualizations with just a few clicks. You can customize
  everything: select items to see, filter and sort them, customize properties, and select how you want
  to view the report.
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="features-slider-wrap">
       <div class="features-slider">
        <div class="slider-list">
         <div class="slider-item">
          <div class="slider-item-pic">
           <svg height="100%" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 200 96" width="100%" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink">
            <title>
             chart-previews

    <section class="feature-content-section sd">
     <article class="content-section">
      <h2>
       Service Desk
      </h2>
      <p class="sub-head">
       Service Desk is a standalone application that allows users without a Targetprocess license to submit any
  kind of requests, search and vote for ideas, add comments, and track the status of related items in
  Targetprocess.
      </p>
      <div class="large-pics">
       <div class="image plate-ico">
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="plates fix-height">

  you need.

        <p>
         Available for both
         <b>
          SaaS
         </b>
         and
         <b>
          On-Premise
         </b>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Targetprocess can integrate with your existing development tools to create a central hub for collaboration and management across your enterprise. Get rid of information islands and standardize your process across your entire organization.
        </p>
        <a class="full-link" href="/integrations">
         Full list of integrations
        </a>
        <div class="sub-block">
         <div class="sub-title">
          More than
         </div>
         <div class="sub-value">
          60 apps
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="benefits">
        <div class="title">
         Benefits
        </div>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <p>
           Consolidate silos of information by connecting your mission critical systems and tools to Targetprocess. Get visibility and traceability with a full history of software changes and data flow in a "single source of truth".
          </p>
         </li>
         <li>
          <p>
           Define rules and configurations that map your processes to your existing tools to ensure a consistent workflow across all your teams. Web-based administration provides the ability to perform field-level mapping, configure custom integration rules, and automate conflict resolution.
          </p>
         </li>
         <li>
          <p>
           And surely don't spend time and money constantly exporting/importing data and configuring multiple independent integration technologies. Increase the ROI on your existing tools by connecting them to Targetprocess.
          </p>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
